<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->2b:T1a8d,<p>India&#8217;s ambitious new electric vehicle (EV) policy aims to transform the automotive landscape, drive self-reliance, and establish the country as a global hub for EV manufacturing. As this policy unfolds, Grade A Industrial Parks, such as those developed by KSH INFRA, are poised to play a crucial role in realising these goals. Here&#8217;s how these state-of-the-art industrial parks contribute to India&#8217;s EV revolution.</p>
<h2>Facilitating Local Manufacturing</h2>
<p>Grade A Industrial Parks provide the necessary infrastructure for EV manufacturers to set up production facilities. These parks offer modern, compliant facilities that include:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Advanced Manufacturing Units:</strong> Designed with high ceilings, wide column spacing, and large floor plates to accommodate large-scale manufacturing operations.</li>
<li><strong>Utilities and Services:</strong> Reliable power, water, waste management systems, and other essential services to ensure seamless operations.</li>
<li><strong>Regulatory Compliance:</strong> Adherence to environmental and safety regulations crucial for manufacturing EVs.</li>
</ul>
<p>These features make these parks ideal for global EV manufacturers like Tesla and VinFast, who are looking to establish a presence in India.</p>
<h2>Supporting Supply Chain Integration</h2>
<p>Industrial parks are not just about providing manufacturing space; they serve as comprehensive hubs for the entire EV supply chain, including:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Component Suppliers:</strong> Housing suppliers of batteries, electric motors, and other critical components.</li>
<li><strong>Integrated Logistics:</strong> Streamlined logistics solutions that reduce costs and improve efficiency.</li>
<li><strong>R&amp;D Facilities:</strong> Encouraging innovation through dedicated spaces for research and development.</li>
</ul>
<p>This integrated approach helps create a robust EV ecosystem, which is essential for sustaining the industry&#8217;s growth.</p>
<h2>Encouraging Investment and FDI</h2>
<p>By offering world-class infrastructure and investment incentives, Grade A Industrial Parks attract both domestic and foreign investments. Key incentives include:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Tax Benefits and Subsidies:</strong> These financial incentives make it attractive for manufacturers to invest in India.</li>
<li><strong>Ease of Setup:</strong> Simplified processes for obtaining clearances and permits, reducing the time and cost of setting up operations.</li>
</ul>
<p>These factors make these parks a magnet for global automakers and investors, further driving the growth of India&#8217;s EV sector.</p>
<h2>Developing Charging Infrastructure</h2>
<p>A significant challenge in the EV ecosystem is the availability of charging infrastructure. Industrial parks address this by:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Installing Charging Stations:</strong> Setting up EV charging stations within the parks to support manufacturing and employee needs.</li>
<li><strong>Battery Swapping Facilities:</strong> Providing battery swapping stations to enhance the convenience and efficiency of EV usage.</li>
</ul>
<p>This infrastructure is vital for the widespread adoption of EVs and supports the government&#8217;s push for sustainable transportation.</p>
<h2>Job Creation and Skill Development</h2>
<p>The establishment of EV manufacturing units in industrial parks leads to substantial job creation and skill development:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Employment Opportunities:</strong> Creation of jobs in manufacturing, logistics, R&amp;D, and other related sectors.</li>
<li><strong>Training Programs:</strong> Offering programs to develop a skilled workforce tailored to the needs of the EV industry.</li>
</ul>
<p>This boosts the local economy and ensures a steady supply of skilled labour for the growing EV market.</p>
<h2>Promoting Environmental Sustainability</h2>
<p>Industrial parks are designed with sustainability in mind, contributing to the green goals of the EV policy by:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Green Buildings:</strong> Using eco-friendly building materials and energy-efficient designs.</li>
<li><strong>Renewable Energy:</strong> Utilising solar and wind power to reduce the carbon footprint of manufacturing operations.</li>
</ul>
<p>By fostering a sustainable manufacturing environment, these parks help address environmental concerns associated with the automotive industry.</p>
<h2>Positioning India as an EV Export Hub</h2>
<p>With their strategic locations and advanced logistics capabilities, Grade A Industrial Parks are well-positioned to make India a hub for EV exports:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Proximity to Ports:</strong> Locations near ports and major transportation networks facilitate easy export of goods.</li>
<li><strong>Customs and Trade Facilitation:</strong> Offering customs bonded warehouses and trade facilitation services to streamline exports.</li>
</ul>
<p>This positions India as a critical player in the global EV market, catering to the growing demand in South Asia and Southeast Asia.</p>
<h2>The Future of EV Manufacturing Is Here</h2>
<p>As we stand on the brink of a new era in manufacturing, Grade A industrial parks are more than just spaces; they are where the future of EV manufacturing is shaped. These facilities, driven by innovation, customization, and a commitment to sustainability, showcase the contribution of industrial parks to setting new standards in the industry. With their advanced infrastructure, integrated supply chain solutions, and sustainable practices, these parks provide the blueprint for success for those aiming to lead in this evolving landscape: innovate, customise, and sustain.</p>
<p>In particular, the Grade A parks in Chakan, Pune, an industrial hub for automobile and automobile components manufacturing, exemplify how industrial infrastructure can support and accelerate the growth of the EV sector in India. These parks are essential in driving the EV revolution, fostering a sustainable and innovative manufacturing environment, and ensuring India&#8217;s position as a critical player in the global automotive industry. The future of EV manufacturing is here, and these industrial parks&#8217; advanced capabilities and visionary planning are shaping it.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->2d:T15c1,<p>Industrial development in India is rapidly evolving, and the emergence of Grade A manufacturing facilities is a pivotal shift towards efficiency and innovation. Defined by their superior infrastructure and strategic design, Grade A facilities are more than just industrial units; they are complex ecosystems designed to support high-level manufacturing operations. Central to their appeal is the concept of space optimization, which is increasingly recognized as essential for operational excellence. In this blog, we delve into the crucial role of space optimization in <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/revolutionising-manufacturing-power-built-to-suit-grade-facilities-0pz9f/" target="blank" rel="noopener">Grade A manufacturing facilities</a>, exploring how state-of-the-art designs and strategic layouts can significantly enhance operational efficiency and profitability.</p>
<h2>Characteristics of Grade A Industrial Parks</h2>
<p>Grade A industrial parks represent the pinnacle of modern manufacturing and logistics infrastructure. Key features include:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Customization and Design Excellence</strong>: Tailored design and customization options play a crucial role in maximizing manufacturing output. These adaptations not only save costs but also minimize the overall infrastructure impact on natural resources. For example, KSH Infra parks are provisioned with special features such as natural sunlight, louvers on each bay, and polycarbonate glass ends at every corner, maximizing air, light, and space for the clients.</li>
<li><strong>Cutting-edge Technology and Strategic Design</strong>: Synonymous with the highest standards in the industry, ensuring facilities are equipped for future challenges.</li>
<li><strong>State-of-the-Art Infrastructure</strong>: Utilizes advanced materials and building techniques to enhance longevity and durability.</li>
<li><strong>Optimal Location</strong>: Carefully selected sites ensure proximity to major transport routes, enhancing logistical efficiency.</li>
<li><strong>Integration of Advanced Technologies</strong>: Ease incorporating the Internet of Things (IoT), artificial intelligence (AI), and automation to streamline operations and boost productivity.</li>
<li><strong>Sustainability Goals</strong>: Designed with environmental sustainability in mind, helping tenants achieve their green objectives through energy-efficient buildings and sustainable practices.</li>
</ul>
<h2>The Blueprint of Efficiency: Space Optimization in Grade A Facilities</h2>
<p>Grade A manufacturing standards are defining the future of industrial spaces. In these facilities, every square inch is optimized to contribute to operational efficiency. Space optimization is critical in these environments, as it directly impacts productivity and operational costs. By maximizing the use of space, companies can minimize waste, reduce the time and effort needed for various manufacturing processes, and streamline workflow.</p>
<h2>Designing Excellence: Grade A Facility Layout Perfection</h2>
<p>In Grade A facilities, the layout is meticulously planned to ensure that every component of the manufacturing process is enhanced for peak performance. This includes optimal aisle spacing to improve accessibility and safety, as well as the strategic placement of equipment to enhance workflow and reduce bottlenecks. Moreover, these facilities are designed with flexibility in mind, allowing for easy reconfiguration of spaces as business needs evolve and technologies advance, ensuring that the facilities remain at the forefront of industry standards.</p>
<h2>Profit Growth: Financial Upside of Grade A Facility</h2>
<p>The financial benefits of operating in a Grade A facility are substantial. Space optimization reduces operational costs and enhances the overall output, acting as a profit multiplier. By leveraging the full potential of Grade A advantages, companies can achieve a leaner manufacturing cycle and a robust bottom line.</p>
<h2>Competitive Advantages Offered by Grade A Facilities</h2>
<p>Beyond space optimization, Grade A facilities offer numerous competitive advantages. They attract top talent by providing a high-quality work environment with modern amenities and technologies. These facilities also foster innovation through collaborative spaces and tech-enhanced areas that encourage creativity and problem-solving. Furthermore, operating out of a Grade A facility significantly enhances a company&#8217;s corporate image, associating the brand with sustainability, innovation, and high standards.</p>
<h2>Conclusion</h2>
<p>The strategic importance of space optimization in Grade A manufacturing facilities cannot be overstated. These facilities are designed to meet current standards and define the <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/fueling-future-manufacturing-enabling-growth-ksh-chakan-park-ohebc/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">future of manufacturing</a> itself. As we look forward to the trends that will shape industrial parks in the coming years, KSH Infra stands out as a leader in the development of <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/grade-a-industrial-parks-like-ksh-chakan-park-iii-are-modernizing-indias-manufacturing-sector-by-providing-eco-friendly-and-efficient-facilities/">Grade A Manufacturing Parks</a>. With a proven track record and a commitment to excellence, <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/">KSH Infra</a> continues to set the benchmark for industrial park development, delivering facilities that are built to last and designed to evolve.</p>

Central to this transformation are modern warehousing solutions that enhance the efficiency and effectiveness of online retail operations. This blog explores the pivotal role of <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/parks/">Grade A warehousing parks</a> in supporting and propelling the e-commerce boom, with a particular focus on how they are engineered to meet the industry&#8217;s modern demands.</p>
<h2>The Rise of E-Commerce in India</h2>
<p>The last decade has seen a dramatic increase in online shoppers in India, a trend underpinned by high internet penetration and the affordability of smartphones and data plans. This digital expansion, as detailed in <a href="https://www.kenresearch.com/industry-reports/india-e-commerce-logistics-market" rel="noopener" target="_blank">KenResearch&#8217;s report</a>, is further bolstered by supportive government initiatives aimed at fostering a tech-savvy marketplace. The convenience of shopping from home has reshaped consumer habits and created a fertile ground for e-commerce to flourish.</p>
<h2>Strategic Importance of Grade A Warehousing Parks</h2>
<p>Grade A warehousing parks are distinguished by their modern infrastructure and strategic placement close to urban centres and major transport hubs. These characteristics are beneficial and essential for e-commerce businesses that promise quick delivery times. Efficient warehousing ensures that orders are processed swiftly, thereby enhancing customer satisfaction and fostering loyalty.</p>
<h2>Technological Integration and Operational Efficiency</h2>
<p>Today&#8217;s Grade A warehousing facilities lay the foundation for integration with state-of-the-art technologies such as IoT, advanced algorithms, and data analytics. These technologies are crucial for optimising inventory management and logistics, ensuring that products are stored systematically and orders are fulfilled quickly. Integrating such advanced systems directly translates into operational efficiency and improved customer experiences.</p>
<h2>Economies of Scale and Cost Efficiency</h2>
<p>The expansive nature of Grade A warehouses allows for the storage of large volumes of goods, which provides significant economies of scale. These facilities often result in reduced operational costs, which can then be passed on to consumers through lower prices. Moreover, their strategic locations minimise transportation costs, further driving down expenses and enhancing the overall competitiveness of e-commerce businesses.</p>
<h2>Sustainability and Security in E-Commerce Logistics</h2>
<p>Sustainability and security are paramount in today&#8217;s warehousing solutions. Grade A facilities are increasingly incorporating green technologies such as solar panels and systems for water conservation, reflecting a commitment to environmental responsibility. Additionally, advanced security measures protect both physical and digital assets, ensuring that these logistics hubs can withstand the challenges of modern threats and vulnerabilities.</p>
<h2>Preparing for Future Growth</h2>
<p>One of the most significant advantages of Grade A warehousing facilities is their scalability. Designed to accommodate rapid growth, these warehouses can expand operations without the need for e-commerce companies to relocate. This aspect is crucial for businesses anticipating quick expansion in line with rising consumer demands and market opportunities.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->33:T1455,<p>The manufacturing landscape is radically transforming, driven by the relentless pursuit of excellence and innovation. In this dynamic environment, the emergence of built-to-suit <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/parks/">Grade A industrial parks</a> is a testament to the industry&#8217;s forward march, offering more than just a space for manufacturing; they are the catalyst for the next wave of the industrial revolution.</p>
<h2>The Essence of Grade A Industrial Parks</h2>
<p>Grade A industrial parks stand at the forefront of this transformation, embodying more than just advanced structures; they are vibrant ecosystems crafted to catalyze innovation, operational efficiency, and expansive growth. These facilities distinguish themselves through several core characteristics:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Advanced Infrastructure</strong>: Integration of cutting-edge technology and infrastructure, ensuring operational excellence and future-readiness.</li>
<li><strong>Safety and Compliance</strong>: Stringent adherence to safety standards and regulatory compliances, providing a secure environment for workers and operations.</li>
<li><strong>Connectivity and Accessibility</strong>: Strategic location choices that offer optimal logistics, connectivity to major transport routes, and accessibility for employees and supplies.</li>
</ol>
<h2>Customization: The Game-Changer</h2>
<p>The real magic, however, lies in the customization of these spaces. Built-to-suit facilities are meticulously tailored to fit the unique requirements of their occupants, ensuring every square foot is optimized for maximum productivity and innovation. This tailored approach paves the way for unparalleled advancements in manufacturing by:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Tailored Design</strong>: Facilities are designed to meet the specific needs of businesses, from floor plans to specialized equipment installations, ensuring maximum efficiency.</li>
<li><strong>Scalability</strong>: Ability to adapt and expand facilities in response to business growth or changing market demands, ensuring long-term viability.</li>
<li><strong>Integration of Innovations</strong>: Custom facilities allow for incorporating the latest industry innovations, from sustainable building materials to smart automation systems.</li>
</ol>
<h2>Success Stories That Inspire</h2>
<p>KSH Infra&#8217;s journey is replete with instances where such specialized environments have not only met but exceeded expectations. Our success stories serve as guiding lights, illuminating the way for others in the industry and demonstrating the tangible benefits of investing in meticulously crafted spaces.</p>
<p><strong>Jabil&#8217;s Custom Facility</strong><br />
KSH Infra developed a tailor-made solution for Jabil, a global manufacturing giant, demonstrating the power of built-to-suit Grade A facilities. This collaboration not only fulfilled Jabil&#8217;s specific operational requirements but also set new benchmarks in efficiency and innovation. To read the full case study, visit <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/jabil/">KSH Infra&#8217;s Jabil Project</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Kawasaki&#8217;s Strategic Expansion</strong><br />
Kawasaki&#8217;s venture with KSH Infra showcases a strategic expansion in India facilitated by a custom-built Grade A facility. This success story highlights how such specialized environments can propel multinational companies towards achieving their growth and operational excellence goals in new markets. Read the full case study at <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/kawasaki/">KSH Infra&#8217;s Kawasaki Project</a>.</p>
<h2>Sustainability: The Cornerstone of Modern Manufacturing</h2>
<p>Incorporating sustainability practices into these facilities is not just an option; it&#8217;s a necessity. KSH Infra&#8217;s commitment to green development is evident in their projects, where eco-friendly practices are not just implemented but are integral to the design and operation, ensuring that the manufacturing processes contribute positively to the environment. This commitment to eco-friendliness is demonstrated through:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Eco-friendly Materials and Practices</strong>: Use of sustainable materials in construction and eco-friendly practices in operations to reduce the carbon footprint.</li>
<li><strong>Energy Efficiency</strong>: Implementation of renewable energy sources, energy-efficient lighting, and HVAC systems that minimize energy consumption.</li>
<li><strong>Waste Reduction and Recycling</strong>: Initiatives for waste reduction, recycling programs, and water conservation underscoring the commitment to environmental stewardship.</li>
</ol>
<h2>The Future Is Here</h2>
<p>As we stand on the brink of a new era in manufacturing, KSH Infra plays a pivotal role with their Grade A industrial parks that are more than just spaces; they are where the future of manufacturing is shaped. These facilities, driven by innovation, customization, and a commitment to sustainability, showcase KSH Infra&#8217;s contribution to setting new standards in the industry. KSH Infra offers the blueprint for success for those aiming to lead in this evolving landscape: innovate, customize, and sustain.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->35:T1478,<h2>Introduction</h2>
<p>In the tapestry of economic development, <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/parks/">Grade A industrial parks</a> are vibrant threads, weaving together opportunities for jobs, growth, and comprehensive societal advancement. These parks are more than just business hubs; they are catalysts for transformation within their respective regions, driving economic, technological, and social progress. This blog delves into the multifaceted socioeconomic impacts of such industrial zones, highlighting their instrumental role in shaping prosperous communities and economies.</p>
<h2>Key Socioeconomic Impacts</h2>
<p><strong>Job Creation</strong><br />
One of the most immediate and visible benefits of Grade A industrial parks is the significant employment opportunities they generate. By attracting a diverse array of businesses, these parks create a demand for a wide range of skills, offering both skilled and unskilled positions that can substantially reduce local unemployment rates. The ripple effect of job creation extends beyond the individual, positively impacting families and communities at large.</p>
<p><strong>Economic Growth</strong><br />
Industrial parks serve as engines of <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/unpacking-indias-industrial-and-logistics-sector-growth-2024-insights-from-ksh-infra/">economic growth</a>, catalyzing the flow of investments and fostering an entrepreneurial ecosystem. The concentration of businesses within these parks stimulates local economies, enhancing the Gross Domestic Product (GDP) and facilitating a thriving economic environment. This growth is not confined to the industrial sector alone; it spills over to ancillary businesses and service providers, contributing to a <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/elevating-indias-industrial-infra-landscape-ksh-infra-ozhkf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">robust economic landscape</a>.</p>
<p><strong>Technology Transfer and Innovation</strong><br />
The aggregation of industries within these parks fosters an environment ripe for innovation and technology transfer. Companies situated in industrial parks often have access to state-of-the-art technology and are part of a network that encourages the exchange of ideas and best practices. This culture of innovation not only enhances the competitiveness of businesses on a global scale but also propels the local industry forward.</p>
<h2>Socioeconomic Impact of Investing in Industrial Areas</h2>
<p><strong>Infrastructure Development</strong><br />
The establishment of industrial parks necessitates the development of essential infrastructure, including transportation networks, utilities, and other facilities. These developments benefit not only the businesses within the parks but also the surrounding communities, improving access to services and enhancing the quality of life.</p>
<p><strong>Community Development and Poverty Alleviation</strong><br />
Investments in industrial parks contribute significantly to community development and poverty alleviation. The creation of jobs provides stable income sources for individuals, lifting families out of poverty and fostering an improved standard of living. Additionally, many industrial parks engage in corporate social responsibility (CSR) initiatives, further supporting the socioeconomic development of nearby areas.</p>
<p><strong>Skills Development</strong><br />
The demand for a skilled workforce within industrial parks leads to increased opportunities for training and education. Businesses often invest in skills development programs, enhancing the employability and productivity of the local workforce. This focus on capacity building ensures that the benefits of industrial growth are sustainable and far-reaching.</p>
<h2>KSH Infra&#8217;s JV with MIDC: A Paradigm of Industrial Synergy</h2>
<p>A shining example of the positive <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/ksh-infras-strategic-impact-shaping-indias-industrial-growth-with-grade-a-infrastructure/">impact of Grade A industrial parks</a> is the joint venture between KSH Infra and the Maharashtra Industrial Development Corporation (MIDC) for a 100-acre development in Talegaon. This collaboration is set to create over 4,000 jobs, inject INR 900 Cr into the local economy and catalyze unprecedented growth in the region. KSH Infra&#8217;s commitment to excellence and <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/sustainability-in-industrial-infrastructure-driving-green-development-at-ksh-infra/">sustainable development</a>, coupled with MIDC&#8217;s strategic vision, promises to transform Maharashtra&#8217;s industrial landscape, offering a brighter future for businesses and communities alike.</p>
<p>Grade A industrial parks are more than just business enclaves; they are beacons of socioeconomic progress, driving job creation, economic growth, and community development. The collaboration between KSH Infra and MIDC in Talegaon is a testament to the transformative power of strategic partnerships in industrial development. As we look to the future, the continued investment in and expansion of industrial parks will undoubtedly play a pivotal role in shaping vibrant, prosperous, and sustainable economies and societies.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->37:T120c,<p>KSH Infra is emerging as a transformative force in the realm of industrial space development in India, playing a pivotal role in the nation&#8217;s industrial advancement. With a strategic focus on developing <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/grade-a-industrial-parks-like-ksh-chakan-park-iii-are-modernizing-indias-manufacturing-sector-by-providing-eco-friendly-and-efficient-facilities/">industrial parks</a>, KSH Infra is not just facilitating the growth of businesses but is also contributing significantly to the broader economic landscape of the country. The company&#8217;s innovative approach to designing and managing industrial spaces sets new benchmarks in the sector.</p>
<h2>Location Advantages</h2>
<p>KSH Infra&#8217;s strategic locations, particularly in Chakan Pune, provide significant connectivity advantages due to their proximity to major transport routes. These locations ensure seamless logistics and access to critical markets. Expanding beyond Pune, KSH Infra plans to establish a PAN India portfolio with <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/parks/">Grade A Logistics and Industrial Parks</a> at strategic locations nationwide, further enhancing their offering to businesses looking for competitive distribution and accessibility advantages.</p>
<h2>Customizable Industrial Spaces</h2>
<p>Understanding the diverse needs of various industries, from manufacturing giants to burgeoning logistics companies, KSH Infra offers highly customisable industrial spaces. These flexible workspace solutions are designed to cater to a wide range of business activities, enabling companies to tailor their operations within these parks according to their specific requirements. This adaptability fosters operational efficiency and encourages innovation within the industrial sector.</p>
<h2>Modern Infrastructure</h2>
<p>At the heart of KSH Infra&#8217;s parks lies state-of-the-art infrastructure equipped with modern facilities and technology-enabled operations. From advanced security systems to high-capacity utilities, the infrastructure is designed to meet international standards, thus enhancing business efficiency and productivity. The integration of smart technologies ensures that the operations are not just efficient but also resilient and scalable, ready to meet the future demands of the industry.</p>
<h2>Sustainability Commitment</h2>
<p>KSH Infra is deeply <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/sustainability-in-industrial-infrastructure-driving-green-development-at-ksh-infra/">committed to sustainability</a>, incorporating green initiatives into every aspect of its park development and operations. The focus on energy-efficient buildings, renewable energy sources, and waste reduction practices underscores the company&#8217;s dedication to minimising the environmental footprint of its industrial parks. These sustainability efforts contribute to global environmental goals and allow businesses to align with green practices, which are increasingly becoming a priority for stakeholders.</p>
<h2>Employee Well-being Amenities</h2>
<p>Recognising that employee well-being is central to business success, KSH Infra&#8217;s industrial parks are equipped with a range of amenities to promote health and recreation among the workforce. From landscaped green spaces to recreational facilities, these amenities create a positive and productive work environment, enhancing employee satisfaction and retention.</p>
<h2>Government and Policy Alignment</h2>
<p>KSH Infra&#8217;s developments are in harmony with the government&#8217;s industrial policies, aligning with initiatives to boost the<a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/ksh-infra-your-trusted-partner-in-automotive-manufacturing-expansion/"> manufacturing sector</a> and enhance the ease of doing business in India. This alignment ensures that businesses operating within KSH Infra&#8217;s parks benefit from supportive regulatory frameworks and incentives, further facilitating growth and expansion.</p>
<p>KSH Infra stands at the forefront of redefining <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/unpacking-indias-industrial-and-logistics-sector-growth-2024-insights-from-ksh-infra/">industrial spaces in India</a>, offering businesses a blend of strategic location advantages, customisable workspaces, and modern infrastructure, all while upholding sustainability and employee well-being. Choosing KSH Infra as a partner for industrial expansion in India offers businesses a unique opportunity to thrive in a dynamic and supportive ecosystem, poised for growth in the rapidly evolving industrial sector of the country.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->39:T1310,<p>India&#8217;s industrial and logistics sector is undergoing a significant transformation, marking an impressive growth trajectory. At KSH Infra, we have been closely monitoring these developments. Our insights aim to shed light on the dynamic factors and emerging trends that are shaping this sector.</p>
<h2>2023 Sector Analysis:</h2>
<p>In 2023, the sector witnessed a remarkable 6.7% increase in absorption, reaching a notable 49 million sq ft. This growth was predominantly seen in Tier I cities, accounting for 75% of this expansion. This statistic underscores the vital role of major urban centers in driving the sector&#8217;s growth.</p>
<h2>Rising Demand in Various Sectors:</h2>
<p>The increase in demand across the sector is multifaceted, primarily driven by key areas such as manufacturing, retail, and third-party logistics (3PL). Government initiatives like &#8216;Make in India&#8217; and the Production Linked Incentive (PLI) scheme have acted as significant catalysts, boosting sectoral growth and enhancing India&#8217;s appeal as a <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/grade-a-industrial-parks-like-ksh-chakan-park-iii-are-modernizing-indias-manufacturing-sector-by-providing-eco-friendly-and-efficient-facilities/">manufacturing and logistics hub</a>.</p>
<h2>Supply Dynamics in 2023:</h2>
<p>The year 2023 also saw a surge in supply, with an addition of 62 million sq ft to the market. Notably, the majority of this new supply, around 75%, originated from Tier I cities. This increase in supply is a direct response to the growing demand and an indicator of the confidence of major developers in the sector&#8217;s potential.</p>
<h2>Evolution of Grade A Spaces:</h2>
<p>The industrial and logistics sector is witnessing a notable shift towards high-quality, compliant infrastructure. In 2023, <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/grade-a-industrial-parks-like-ksh-chakan-park-iii-are-modernizing-indias-manufacturing-sector-by-providing-eco-friendly-and-efficient-facilities/">Grade A spaces</a>, known for their superior standards and amenities, accounted for 53% of the total market supply, a significant increase from 48% in the previous year. This trend highlights an increasing preference for premium, well-equipped spaces, reflecting a maturing market and evolving customer expectations.</p>
<h2>Forecast for 2024 and Beyond:</h2>
<p>Looking ahead, the growth trajectory for India&#8217;s industrial and logistics sector appears robust. The 3PL and manufacturing sectors, in particular, are poised to drive this expansion. We anticipate the absorption rate to exceed 13%, with supply growth potentially surpassing 14%. This optimistic forecast is underpinned by the continued evolution of the sector and supportive governmental policies.</p>
<h2>E-commerce Impact on Warehousing:</h2>
<p>E-commerce has been a game changer for the warehousing segment. Its influence extends beyond traditional urban centers, stimulating significant growth in Tier II and III cities. The sector&#8217;s contribution to warehousing and logistics is set to see a considerable increase, a testament to the expanding reach and innovative business models of <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/the-distinction-between-grade-a-and-stantard-warehouses-what-e-commerce-industry-needs-to-know/">e-commerce</a> companies. This trend underscores the evolving landscape of Indian warehousing, transitioning from conventional storage solutions to more advanced, technology-driven facilities.</p>
<h2>Regional Highlights and Trends:</h2>
<p>Delhi-NCR, Mumbai, Bengaluru, and Pune have emerged as the powerhouses in the industrial and logistics sector, contributing significantly to the overall growth. However, the momentum is wider than these metros. We are witnessing a gradual but definitive shift towards other urban and semi-urban areas. This expansion diversifies the sector&#8217;s geographic footprint, indicating a more inclusive growth pattern across the country.</p>
<h2>Future of Rental Values:</h2>
<p>In the coming year, we expect a marginal rise in rental values for compliant buildings. This increase, however, will vary based on location, reflecting the differing regional dynamics and demand patterns.</p>
<h3>Conclusion:</h3>
<p>India&#8217;s industrial and logistics sector is on the brink of a transformative phase. With rapid growth, evolving market dynamics, and increasing diversification, stakeholders must stay informed and agile. Adapting to these changes will be vital to capitalizing on the opportunities this sector presents.</p>
<p>At <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/">KSH Infra</a>, we are at the forefront of understanding and adapting to these trends. For more insights and to explore collaboration opportunities, we invite you to connect with us and join in shaping the future of India&#8217;s industrial and logistics landscape.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->3b:Te15,<p>The e-commerce industry&#8217;s rapid growth has brought an increasing demand for warehousing solutions. As companies strive to optimize their supply chains, the choice of warehouse grade becomes crucial. This article will explore the key differences between Grade A and Stantard warehouses and their implications for e-commerce businesses.</p>
<h2>Infrastructure &amp; Construction Quality</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Grade A Warehouses: </strong> These facilities are the pinnacle of modern warehousing, built to international standards. They boast high ceilings suitable for modern racking systems and are equipped to handle heavy machinery. Their construction quality is top-notch, ensuring durability and longevity.</li>
<li><strong>Standard Warehouses:</strong> Often older, these warehouses might need more of the refinements of their Grade A counterparts. They serve the purpose but may need to be optimized for the latest warehousing practices.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Location</h2>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">
<ul>
<li><strong>Grade A:</strong> These warehouses are strategically located and ensure quick access to major transport routes, urban centres, and other logistical hubs.</li>
<li><strong>Standard:</strong> These might be situated farther from key areas, potentially leading to longer transportation times and increased costs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Facilities &amp; Amenities</h2>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">
<ul>
<li><strong>Grade A:</strong> With state-of-the-art facilities, these warehouses might offer temperature control, advanced fire safety systems, and efficient loading docks. They also consider the well-being of workers with amenities like canteens.</li>
<li><strong>Standard:</strong> While functional, they might lack some advanced facilities, making them less versatile for diverse storage needs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Technology Integration</h2>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">
<ul>
<li><strong>Grade A:</strong> Seamlessly integrated with modern tech solutions, these warehouses offer advanced inventory management and security systems.</li>
<li><strong>Standard:</strong> They might serve basic storage needs but could lag in technological integration.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Maintenance &amp; Upkeep</h2>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">
<ul>
<li><strong>Grade A:</strong> Regular maintenance ensures these warehouses remain in optimal condition, safeguarding goods and ensuring smooth operations.</li>
<li><strong>Standard:</strong> The level of upkeep might vary, potentially leading to wear and tear over time.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Implications for E-commerce</h2>
<p>For e-commerce businesses, the choice of warehouse can impact efficiency, costs, scalability, reputation, and the ability to cater to specialized storage needs. While <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/parks/">Grade A warehouses</a> come with a higher price tag, their advantages, especially in terms of efficiency and scalability, can significantly outweigh the costs for growing e-commerce businesses.</p>
<p>As the e-commerce industry continues to evolve, the choice of warehousing solutions will play a pivotal role in determining operational efficiency, customer satisfaction, and overall growth. Whether opting for Grade A or a standard warehouse, businesses must weigh their specific needs, budgets, and growth projections to make an informed decision.</p>
<p><strong>Join hands with <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/contact-us/">KSH INFRA</a> and make an informed, sustainable choice for your e-commerce warehousing needs!</strong></p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->3d:T1b86,<p>The Indian manufacturing sector stands at a pivotal point, poised to embrace modernity and efficiency like never before. Amidst this transformative phase,<a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/parks/"> Grade A industrial parks</a> are emerging as the linchpins driving this change. KSH Chakan Park III, the latest and one of the largest developments in Chakan, Pune, exemplifies this transformation. As an eco-conscious and sustainable warehousing and industrial park, it sets new standards in operational efficiency, safety, and <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/ksh-infra-powering-indias-green-automotive-revolution-esg-compliant">green industrial development</a>. Soon to be IGBC Platinum certified, it reflects KSH Infra&#8217;s unwavering commitment to sustainable progress.</p>
<h2>Understanding Grade A Industrial Parks</h2>
<p>Grade A industrial parks represent the pinnacle in industrial infrastructure, offering world-class amenities, robust security, and unparalleled operational efficiency. Unlike their Grade B and C counterparts, these parks are meticulously planned and feature top-notch facilities that cater to the diverse needs of modern manufacturing units. They serve as the backbone for industries aiming to thrive in today&#8217;s competitive landscape.</p>
<h2>Operational Efficiency and Advanced Amenities</h2>
<p><a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/ksh-chakan-iii/">KSH Chakan Park III</a> stands out as a Grade A industrial park, offering unparalleled operational efficiency vital for modern industrial operations.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Wide Roads for Easy Accessibility:</strong> The park features 15m wide bitumen roads, ensuring easy manoeuvrability for trucks and smooth transportation of goods.</li>
<li><strong>Secured Entry and Exit Points:</strong> Motorized entrance gates equipped with boom barriers facilitate secure and efficient entry and exit within the park.</li>
<li><strong>Comprehensive Surveillance:</strong> A CCTV system is installed throughout the park, enhancing security and monitoring operations.</li>
<li><strong>Optimal Ventilation:</strong> The park is designed to facilitate 6-8 air changes, ensuring a well-ventilated work environment.</li>
<li><strong>Accommodating Structure Design:</strong> With a clear height ranging from 9-12m from the Finished Floor Level (FFL), the park can accommodate various industrial needs.</li>
<li><strong>Reliable Power Backup:</strong> A 100% DG backup ensures that external lighting and common services remain operational at all times.</li>
<li><strong>Advanced Firefighting Systems:</strong> The park is equipped with sprinkler-based systems, smoke detectors, and beam detectors for fire safety.</li>
<li><strong>Efficient Lighting:</strong> The buildings within the park are illuminated with 150 lux LED lights, ensuring a bright and productive work environment.</li>
<li><strong>Well-Planned Water Systems:</strong> Stormwater drains are strategically placed throughout the park to prevent flooding and maintain smooth operations.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Robust Safety Measures</h2>
<p>KSH Chakan Park III prioritizes safety, which remains paramount in any industrial setting, and Grade A parks set the standard.</p>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">
<ul>
<li><strong>Perimeter Security:</strong> The park is secured with a compound wall and fencing along the perimeter, ensuring a protected work environment.</li>
<li><strong>Surveillance for Safety:</strong> The comprehensive CCTV system monitors activities within the park, enhancing security and safety.</li>
<li><strong>Fire Safety Measures:</strong> Equipped with a sprinkler-based firefighting system, smoke detectors, and beam detectors, the park ensures a rapid response in case of fire emergencies.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Sustainability and Eco-Friendly Practices</h2>
<p>Sustainability is at the heart of Grade A industrial parks. KSH Chakan Park III embodies the commitment to eco-friendly and <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/blogs/sustainability-in-industrial-infrastructure-driving-green-development-at-ksh-infra/">sustainable industrial development.</a></p>
<ul>
<li style="list-style-type: none;">
<ul>
<li><strong>Rainwater Harvesting:</strong> The park employs rainwater harvesting systems, contributing to water conservation and sustainability.</li>
<li><strong>Water Recycling:</strong> Water is recycled using a Sewage Treatment Plant (STP), promoting efficient water use.</li>
<li><strong>Green Spaces:</strong> Extensive landscaping in common areas enhances the park&#8217;s aesthetics and contributes to a greener environment.</li>
<li><strong>Signage for Navigation:</strong> External and internal signage, including pylons and directional signs, facilitate easy navigation within the park.</li>
<li><strong>Sustainable Infrastructure:</strong> The park&#8217;s infrastructure is built to the highest international standards, ensuring quality and sustainability.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Impact on the Manufacturing Sector</h2>
<p>Grade A industrial parks are revolutionizing India&#8217;s manufacturing sector. By providing state-of-the-art facilities, robust safety measures, and a commitment to sustainability, they are setting new standards and driving innovation. KSH Chakan Park III, situated in the burgeoning industrial hub of Chakan, Pune, is at the forefront of this transformation. With major automobile manufacturers and a growing talent pool in proximity, it plays a crucial role in shaping the future of manufacturing in India.</p>
<h2>Future Outlook</h2>
<p>The future of Grade A industrial parks is bright, with trends pointing towards continuous innovation and <a href="https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/ksh-infra-committed-sustainable-industrial-infrastructure-ksh-infra">sustainable development</a>. Manufacturing units looking to stay ahead of the curve must embrace these changes, leveraging the advanced facilities and eco-friendly practices that parks like KSH Chakan Park III offer.</p>
<p>Grade A industrial parks are the future of manufacturing, offering unparalleled efficiency, safety, and sustainability. KSH Chakan Park III stands as a testament to this future, setting new benchmarks in industrial infrastructure. As the manufacturing sector continues to evolve, embracing these parks is not just an option but a necessity for growth and modernization.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->41:T1375,<p>At KSH INFRA, we understand the world&#8217;s dire need for a sustainable future—a responsibility that extends to all industries, including ours. In our pursuit to create sustainable industrial infrastructure, the recognition we&#8217;ve achieved serves not only to validate our efforts but also to mark our contribution to a greener industrial future. The stringent standards we&#8217;ve adhered to and the certifications we&#8217;ve attained convey our unwavering commitment to sustainable development.</p>
<p>As we delve deeper into our sustainability practices, we invite you to observe firsthand how KSH INFRA equally encompasses ambition and responsibility in fostering green development. Our steadfast commitment towards significantly reducing environmental impact while developing state-of-the-art warehouses and industrial parks is not merely a strategic initiative but a testament to our resolve to ensure sustainable development at the heart of our operations.</p>
<h2>The Need for Sustainability</h2>
<p>Industrial infrastructure plays a critical role in greenhouse gas emissions. KSH INFRA acknowledges this reality and has made intentional strides towards sustainable warehousing—better for businesses, the environment, and ultimately humanity.</p>
<h2>Inside a KSH INFRA Green Warehouse</h2>
<p>We optimise energy use with efficient lighting and equipment; our use of LEDs and motion sensors epitomises this. Our warehouses use sustainable materials designed to improve air quality. We adopt stringent recycling and waste management practices while ensuring safety and adherence to best-in-class amenities.</p>
<h2>The Green Warehouse Exterior</h2>
<p>Our sustainable practices extend beyond our building walls. We incorporate rainwater harvesting and solar panels, while reflective roofing material boosts our energy efficiency. Moreover, we strategically position shade-bearing trees for natural cooling.</p>
<h2>Infrastructure Planning for Sustainability</h2>
<p>KSH INFRA&#8217;s industrial parks are strategically positioned to reduce transportation emissions. We develop brownfield sites, bring benefits to communities, and leverage current infrastructure for sustainability. With local authorities, we ensure an eco-friendly approach towards development, fostering positive social impact and creating employment opportunities.</p>
<h2>The Impacts of Our Green Development</h2>
<p>Our unwavering commitment to sustainability is validated by the IGBC Platinum certification in progress and the prestigious EDGE certification for <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/ksh-chakan-ii/">Chakan Park II Industrial Park</a>. These accomplishments showcase our dedication to creating responsible infrastructure, fostering a green industrial future, and upholding our position as a leader in sustainable development.</p>
<h2>Sustainability Certifications Validate Our Commitment</h2>
<p>Our sustainable efforts result in environmental benefits and carbon footprint reduction. Communities and ecosystems around our facilities enjoy positive effects, while we achieve cost savings. Our brand reputation gets a boost, attracting eco-conscious clients.</p>
<p>Our commitment to green practices is proven by the Indian Green Building Council&#8217;s (IGBC) Platinum certification in progress for our <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/ksh-chakan-iii/">Chakan Park III Industrial Park</a>. As stated by IGBC—a wing of the Confederation of Indian Industry (CII)—, its mission aligns with ours: to develop a sustainable built environment for all. The certification is a testament to our rigorous pursuit of innovation and improvement in our infrastructure.</p>
<p>Adding another accolade to our sustainability efforts, Chakan Park II has received the EDGE certification (Excellence in Design for Greater Efficiency). Being a globally recognised standard adopted in over 150 countries, EDGE ensures resource-efficient and sustainable infrastructure—perfectly aligned with our sustainability objectives.</p>
<h2>Future Goals &amp; Commitment</h2>
<p>Driven by innovation, we aim to expand our green initiatives across all our future parks. We intend to rally our partners towards a collective sustainable <a href="https://www.kshinfra.com/sustainability/">impact—aligning with global sustainability frameworks and goals</a>.</p>
<h2>Conclusion</h2>
<p>In conclusion, our green achievements underline our commitment to sustainability—a crusade we heartily invite other industrial developers to join. After all, green development is key to a sustainable future.</p>
<p>At KSH INFRA, we stand as a beacon of hope setting the pace in sustainability. Our ethos ties us to the future, and our dedication keeps us focused. Navigating the challenges, we remain unabashed in our commitment to delivering high-quality, efficient, sustainable industrial parks. We are not just building warehouses and industrial parks but shaping a future that generations will be proud of.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->44:Tad3,<h2>TALEGAON MIDC PUNE,<br />
A NEW INDUSTRIAL WORLD IN THE MAKING.</h2>
<p>Talegaon in Pune is an upcoming industrial and warehousing neighborhood. With close proximity to Chakan, the region is home to some of the largest engineering companies such as JCB, General Motors, L&amp;T, POSCO, Emerson, PERI and Continental. This location has attracted engineering talent in abundance. A healthy diaspora of talented individuals from across India and from far corners of the globe, makes Talegaon a preferred destination for auto makers and other diverse industries alike. The region is in close proximity to the Port of JNPT in Mumbai and is within striking distance of Mumbai Metropolitan Region.</p>
<h2>TALEGAON MIDC INFRASTRUCTURE</h2>
<p>Talegaon is an emerging warehousing destination in India due to its proximity to all major highways connecting the State of Maharashtra. MIDC (Maharashtra Regional Development Corporation) has large plans for the region, and the total development planned in the area will exceed 10,000 acres when fully completed. Talegoan has already established itself as a self-sufficient residential domain with several residential complexes, hospitals, schools, colleges and restaurants. A large number of Talegaon residents work in the manufacturing and IT domains.</p>
<h2>TALEGAON MIDC CONNECTIVITY</h2>
<p>One of the main advantages of Talegaon MIDC is that it is located just off the Pune-Mumbai highway which ensures quick connectivity to Mumbai International Airport, Jawaharlal Nehru Port Trust (JNPT) and the upcoming Navi Mumbai International Airport. This makes international trade and logistics very convenient. Major industrial belts like Pimpri-Chinchwad Industrial Area and Chakan Industrial Area are directly connected to Talegaon MIDC via a network of well-developed roads. This also makes the movement of trucks and other heavy vehicles very easy. The renowned Hinjawadi IT Park is within a short driving distance.</p>
<p><strong>KEY DISTANCES</strong><br />
Chakan MIDC- 11 Km<br />
PCMC Industrial Area- 25 Km<br />
Mumbai-Pune Expressway- 8 Km<br />
Pune City- 40 Km<br />
Pune Airport- 45 Km<br />
Navi Mumbai- 100 Km<br />
JNPT Sea Port- 100 Km<br />
Navi Mumbai International Airport- 105 Km</p>
<h2>INDUSTRIAL PARK IN TALEGAON MIDC BY KSH INFRA</h2>
<p>Talegaon Park 1, the first infrastructure park by KSH Infra, is a small scale development with 2 standalone structures spanning 1,40,952 SQ FT. Though a boutique venture, nothing about the park is ordinary. Grade-A facilities, be it the construction, security, internal roads or amenities, have led to the success of this park and resulted in KSH Infra attracting some of the largest global investors to its platform like JCB, Renault, Klingspor and Unisource.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->46:Td3e,<p>Pune is no alien territory for MNCs. Over the last decade, the number of German companies in Pune have doubled from 150 to 300 with leading names like Mercedes-Benz, Volkswagen and Bosch among them. Pune is a multi-industrial hub dominated by the automobile and ancillary companies. Over the last few years, new sectors like electronics, bio-technology and high-tech manufacturing are coming up rapidly. It is no secret that establishing manufacturing plants, warehouses and associated infrastructure costs exorbitant amounts of money and demands heavy paperwork. Considering these factors, majority of manufacturers, both Indian and global, have opted for the more cost efficient and hassle-free option of renting out ready-to-move industrial spaces.</p>
<p>Let’s explore some of the key benefits of exercising this option.</p>
<h2>CAPITAL EXPENDITURE VS OPERATING EXPENSES</h2>
<p>During the start-up phase of operations, a company’s business plan is always under the clouds of uncertainty. They are generally new to the market/country and hence have little knowledge of how they would ramp up, and to mitigate the unforeseen risks they tend to go for a lease option. Many companies prefer ready-to-move facilities against incurring heavy capital expenditure in the initial years of operations, as it is easier on their balance sheet.</p>
<h2>LAND ACQUISITION</h2>
<p>Land acquisition issues are plenty in India and large multinational companies have struggled to get the right land parcel clear of all encumbrances in India. This has been a major pain point for most companies looking to set up operations in India, and hence leasing option is being looked at favourably.</p>
<h2>MULTIPLE ESTABLISHMENTS</h2>
<p>Companies are looking to set up more than one plant, and the concept of setting up mother plants is no longer as prevalent as in the past. Nowadays companies are setting up smaller plants close to the consumer markets. Ramping up operations across multiple leased facilities across a market as geographically diverse as India is also far easier than setting up company owned facilities, due to which they are choosing a leasing option.</p>
<h2>GRADE-A DEVELOPERS &amp; FACILITIES</h2>
<p>Grade-A industrial parks offer global standard features, infrastructure and security. Wealth of A-grade developers in India has given multinational companies more options to choose from, and It has now become the norm for companies to evaluate both leased and owned options when taking decisions.</p>
<h2>AMENITIES</h2>
<p>Smaller multinational companies also prefer going to an Industrial park due to various amenities that are available, and costs being lower as opposed to setting up standalone facilities. The concept of setting up standalone utilities as opposed to using park level ones, also impacts overall costs and multinational companies are now becoming more and more aware of these added features that are available at larger industrial parks. Multi-client facilities offer shared resources that reduce operational costs.</p>
<p>With all the advantages that ready-to-move industrial parks offer, why should a company be burdened by unnecessary expenses incurred in building its own facility? KSH Infra has provided several Grade-A industrial spaces to clients like Kawasaki, Kimberley Clark, JCB, Bosch and many more in Pune, and the numbers are only increasing.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->48:Td49,<h2>A COLLABORATION<br />
FOR A GREENER WORLD.</h2>
<p>Rapid development, growing population and urbanization trends are resulting in rapid real estate development across various sectors, be it residential, commercial or industrial. Most of this development is seen in emerging markets and India is one of them. Existing buildings today consume 40 percent of the total electricity globally and generate 19 percent of energy-related GHG emissions. Year on year, pressure on the environment is growing and sustainable development is the only way forward. Currently, green building is not mandatory and hence only a handful of buildings are certified as green. Developers and consumers are not aware of the financial benefits of resource-efficient and sustainable buildings. To embrace greener development systems, resource-efficient building practices must be introduced and implemented. Green construction can reduce emissions, save building material and conserve water &amp; energy for decades.</p>
<p>Even if one wishes to develop sustainable buildings, how would one know the exact requirements to achieve this? Is there a governing law or mandate that states what exactly is necessary? Can an existing building be transformed into a sustainable building? Although many such complex questions may arise while considering green building initiatives, the answer is simple…</p>
<h2>EXCELLENCE IN DESIGN FOR GREATER EFFICIENCIES</h2>
<p>EDGE is an online platform, a green building standard and a certification system. The EDGE application helps to determine the most cost-effective options for designing green within a local climate context. EDGE can be used for buildings of all vintages, including new construction, existing buildings and major retrofits. EDGE is a unique innovation of IFC (INTERNATIONAL FINANCE CORPORATION), member of the World Bank Group. It has already been adopted in over 150 countries. EDGE was created with the intent to offer a simplistic and yet measurable solution to make a positive business case for building green.</p>
<p><strong>KSH</strong> is an organization that does not shy away from accepting change or learning new ways. After developing a couple of industrial parks, the core leadership at KSH realized the need for green building, given the amount of resources that are consumed every day. We have pledged to adopt and implement sustainable development in all ongoing and future developments. Now equipped with the EDGE Certification, we are on a mission to develop highly efficient and sustainable industrial and warehousing infrastructure. KSH Chakan Park 2 is one of only few industrial parks across Pune that offer ecologically <strong>sustainable infrastructure.</strong> At present, all buildings within Chakan Park 2 have been preliminarily assessed and certified by EDGE. The projected savings are quite impressive and will drastically reduce environmental pressure. In addition to this, it will also shrink operational costs and benefit clients. KSH would also execute a massive plantation drive with over a <strong>1000 trees</strong> planted within the premises by team members and leaders alike to create a fresh and aesthetically appealing work environment.</p>
<p>India, being on the verge of becoming a global power, all industries owe it to the future generations to develop responsibly and we at KSH are committed to playing our part.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->4a:Tc43,<p>KSH Multi Modal Logistics &#038; Industrial Parks are designed and built from the groups experience in managing complex logistics operations, building and operating Inland Container Depots. KSH parks offer Grade-A infrastructure in the form of built-to-suit and customisable buildings as per client requirements. The park features and facilities lay a great impetus on environmental sustainability, well planned layout with wide roads for easy maneuverability of trucks, adequate parking spaces, high ceilings, large column spacing for logistics as well as manufacturing companies, water and electricity, sewage treatment plants, effluent treatment plants, office blocks, canteens etc.</p>
<p>KSH Chakan Park 2 is divided into 2 different parks, Park-A and Park-B. These 2 parks all together have 5 buildings named A1, A2, A3, B1 &#038; B2 out of which 2 have received the EDGE ADVANCED PRELIMINARY CERTIFICATE and 3 have received EDGE PRELIMINARY CERTIFICATE.</p>
<h2>LET’S VIEW THE MAIN FACTORS THAT EDGE CONSIDERS ESSENTIAL FOR A BUILDING TO QUALIFY AS SUSTAINABLE.</h2>
<p><strong>ENERGY</strong><br />
Buildings by nature are energy intensive, even a small amount of saving can go a long way and make a substantial impact. EDGE being developed for emerging economies focuses on primary issues, energy consumption being one of the priorities amongst them.</p>
<p>All the projects part of the Chakan Park have been designed to save on massive amounts of energy consumption. This has increased the capital cost very marginally, however, the saving in the operational cost is substantial as compared to a non-EDGE certified building of similar proportion.</p>
<p><strong>WATER</strong><br />
Water would qualify as one of the most critical factors to the life force, however, an infinitely misused resource at the same time. We have regularly been facing draughts every year in various regions of the Indian subcontinent and it is our moral responsibility to take conscious steps towards conserving water.<br />
Something as simple as a low flow faucet can potentially save 50% of water consumption (through taps for hand wash or dish wash)</p>
<p><strong>EMBODIED ENERGY IN MATERIALS</strong><br />
The environmental impacts of materials vary according to where and how they are manufactured, processed and used. Due to the global scope of EDGE, the data for embodied energy of construction materials based on a life cycle assessment (LCA) model. A complex combination of many processed materials determines a building’s total embodied energy.</p>
<p>Some of the sustainability features at KSH Chakan Park 2 include optimised window to wall ratio, Energy saving light bulbs – LED, Water efficient – faucets, urinals, Water closets, Black water recycling in which the recycled water will be used for flushing &#038; landscaping purposes. Use of fly ash bricks &#038; AAC blocks for internal &#038; external walls, Aluminium window frames. Since there is no local municipal water supply to the Industrial area where the warehouses are located borewell water will be used for purposes other than flushing &#038; landscaping.</p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->4c:Tbd9,<p>The COVID-19 pandemic has disrupted every single industry over the course of just a few months. It has completely changed human life, irrespective of demographics, profession and social status. Many of our habits have changed. Our lifestyle, social connect and work culture have mutated beyond reckoning. While economic slowdown brews on one end, new trends are evolving on the other. A new world is emerging…one that might finally accept that ‘abnormal’ is the ‘new normal’.</p>
<p>While world economies were shaken by the Coronavirus, many industries in India took a hit as well. Lower production, pay reduction and high job &#038; business uncertainty have been spooking every tax paying citizen ever since the onset of the pandemic. But in some sectors, the results are exponentially positive. So adaptability and creative decision making will play a key role in the future sustainability of enterprises.</p>
<p>Many countries, including India, have started resuming work in a tamed environment. India could potentially lead the change in a post-Covid world with its vast array of engineers and investment opportunities, according to billionaire entrepreneur Mark Cuban. India could be the next biggest global exporter as many countries are looking to shift operations and this is a real opportunity for diversification for India. In such a case, manufacturing companies in India must quickly adapt to the global demands, diversify their supply chain and focusing on product quality. Every sector will have to reinvent itself to survive in a post-COVID-19 world order.<br />
Several companies that incorporated the work-from-home system have now decided to continue it even post lockdown. From delivering work stations to providing high speed internet connectivity, every company working in the digital and tech space has ensured a smooth transition of work culture. This has not just saved on operational costs but also increased productivity. Such transition may never be possible in the manufacturing sectors, however, innovative systems may be designed to enhance processes that do not require physical presence.</p>
<p>India has become the new land of opportunities as foreign companies look to shift base out of other asian counties and into India. As entrepreneurs, we must work along with our government to create internationally acclaimed benchmarks in manufacturing and distribution to portray reliability and attract foreign investments. Expanding domestic capacity and capability in a strategic manner can make all the difference. With a youth population of nearly 230 million, man power and skilled labour can serve as our greatest strengths.</p>
<p><strong>In summary, manufacturing companies need to articulate a measurable roadmap to increase their current domestic value addition. A strategic approach, technological enhancement, skill development and precise market forecast are some of the key focus areas to make India the next preferred global industrial destination post COVID-19.</strong></p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->4e:T9cf,<p>If you can remember one life-threatening situation that you were in, you already know the importance of being safe. Not every hazardous situation is caused by humans. Some occur naturally. It therefore our moral responsibility to create a safe domestic and professional environment.</p>
<p>Safety is one of the most undermined issues in today’s time. Often people prefer comfort to safety, which eventually leads to horrifying accidents. The best examples of these are not wearing a helmet or seat belts. Though everyone is well aware of the consequences of taking unnecessary risks with their lives, they tend to ignore them and proceed anyway, only to regret later. People forget that safety is not an option but a requirement. Above all, our carefree attitude may jeopardize the safety of others. Not to mention the many lives that subsequently get affected.</p>
<p>Over the past decade, the government and several leading organisations have created strict safety compliance norms, not just related to work, but also at a social level. Even the ongoing COVID19 pandemic has just one major cure – safety and precaution. This week, the entire nation is celebrating ‘National Safety Week’ to create awareness and instil a sense of responsibility in every citizen. KSH Infra has joined this initiative and each employee is playing his or her part in spreading the message. KSH Infra has developed several industrial spaces, some of which have been naturally challenging and demanding. However, at no point has the safety compliance been defied or compromised for convenience. Our safety protocols include the use of helmets, safety goggles, hand gloves, face shields, safety nets, jackets, breathing masks etc. and apply to all those who step onto our premises. Over the past 7 years, we have engaged a workforce of more than 5000 men and women who have worked for millions of hours without a single reported accident and we aim at maintaining the streak. We have recently taken a step further towards safer futures, not just for people, but also the environment.</p>
<p><strong>Our ongoing industrial park at Chakan comprises of EDGE certified green buildings that reduce the pressure on the environment and conserve natural resources. Our endeavours have been a success due to the diligent and sincere efforts of our team and we could not thank them enough for this.</p>
<p>This week, we light the beacon of safety, but let us promise ourselves to keep the torch burning till eternity.</strong></p>

<!-- / Yoast SEO plugin. -->50:Tcdb,<p>There is no debating the fact that modern buildings put tremendous pressure on the environment. Existing buildings today consume 40 percent of the total electricity globally and generate 19 percent of energy-related GHG emissions. It is therefore essential to adopt green building techniques. As human life came to a halt due to the COVID-19 pandemic, the earth initiated a self-healing process. Cleaner water, clearer skies, low seismic activities and the influx of wildlife into human habitats are clear indicators of how rapid development was hampering the existence of our natural world and that nature does not need to be saved, only preserved. When the world resumes, we should remember what we owe our planet and embrace a sustainable future.</p>
<p>KSH Chakan Park 2 is among only a few industrial parks in Pune that offer ecologically sustainable infrastructure. All 5 buildings within the park have been preliminarily assessed and certified by Excellence In Design For Greater Efficiencies (EDGE). The projected savings would not just cut down on the pressure that is building on the environment each day, but also reduce operational costs drastically. In addition to this, KSH would also be planting over 1000 trees within the premises to create a fresh and aesthetically appealing work environment.</p>
<h2>LET US BRIEFLY UNDERSTAND HOW KSH INFRA’S SUSTAINABLE INDUSTRIAL PARKS CAN BENEFIT YOU AS AN END USER.</h2>
<p><strong>Reduced Operational Costs</strong><br />
Green buildings are designed to enable maximum illumination through natural light during the day, while low consumption LED lights are installed to fill-in when required. Similarly, water-efficient urinals and faucets optimize the use of water with little to no wastage. This results in significant savings through reduced energy and water bills over the life of the building.</p>
<p><strong>Refreshing Workspaces</strong><br />
Ample natural light and ventilation within buildings would create a pleasant and healthy indoor environment for the building occupants. As mentioned above, over a 1000 trees would be planted within the premises of the park, which in turn would result in a lush green and refreshing outdoor ambience. This is likely to improve the productivity of employees and benefit the organisation.</p>
<p><strong>Improved Social Image</strong><br />
Manufacturing companies often come under scrutiny due to high emission and energy consumption which many environmentalists and social activists criticize. Consumer behavior is largely affected by a brand’s reputation and its empathy towards the environment. We often see individuals praising or slating organizations for their ethical responsiveness. Moving into a sustainable industrial park exudes a company’s responsibility towards the environment and places it above blatant profiteering firms, thus creating higher value for investors and consumers alike.<br />
Building a sustainable facility is no easy task. Besides procuring land and securing permissions, a proficient team of engineers, architects and technicians with experience in green building must be assigned to the task. So why bother with all the hassles? Opt for a ready to move <strong>sustainable industrial park</strong> developed by KSH Infra at Chakan Pune.</p>
